--- صفحة 26 ---
HOW TO SET-UP YOUR
PRO EMAILS
IMAP {(Internet Message Access Protocol)
Receives and syncs emails across multiple devices.
Stores emails on the server, so you can access them
from anywhere.
Any action (read, delete, move) is reflected across all
connected devices.
SMTP (Simple Mail Transfer Protocol)
Sends emails from your email client to the recipient’s
server.
Does not store emails—it only transfers them.
Requires authentication (email & password) for
security.

. ﻮ ﺿ ﺮ ﺑ ﺎ ﺗ ا ﺪ ﻟ ﺎ ﺑ ﻞ ﻳ ﺎ ﺑ ﻮ ﻤ ﻟ ا ﻖ ﻳ ﺮ ﻃ ﻦ ﻋ
⚠ NOTE:
Most People Fail Because of Content — Not Setup
Even if everything technical is done right, the content strategy is what
makes or breaks your account.
👉 Each account — especially on the same platform — should focus on
a different type of content to avoid overlap and boost reach.
Example Breakdown:
Account 1: Reactions
Acc ount 2: Motivational clips
Account 3: Educational/value-based content
✅ This makes each account unique, engaging a wider range of
audience types while staying within the same personal brand.
--- صفحة 51 ---
Step-by-Step Instructions
✅ 1. Plan Branding & Naming for Each Account
Start by choosing a username and content angle for each account.
Each account — even on the same platform — should have a unique
content focus.
Examples of account styles:
Moosama-Clips → Reaction videos
Moosama-Talks → Motivational content
Best of Mo Osama → Educational or high-value tips
Moosama-Lifestyle → Daily routines, behind-the-scenes
Moosama-Mindset → Self-improvement clips
Moosama-Network → Interviews, networking clips
✅ 2. Prepare Platform-Specific Emails
Use a separate email for each Platform. {OPTIONAL}
Keep access to every email for verification purposes.
✅ 3. Create the Account
Open the account using the assigned email.
Set Your Different username, bio, and profile picture based on the
branding plan.
✅ 4. Configure Account Settings
Change the country/region to suit the audience.
Go to settings:
Add and verify phone number
Add and verify email
Switch from personal to business account
--- صفحة 55 ---
Step 1: Don’t Rush It
New account? Wait.
For the first 1–2 days, don’t post anything.
Just behave like a normal user:
1
Watch videos.
Like some (5–10 per session).
Leave a few genuine comments.
Follow 1–5 creators in your niche.
Repeat this activity daily for at least 2 days or from beginning of open the
account (30+ minutes per day)
Step 2: Stay Inside Your Niche
Engage ONLY with content related to your niche.
If you're planning to post:
2
Fitness content? Watch fitness clips.
Finance tips? Interact with finance creators.
Comedy or reactions? Stick with those.
This tells what kind of content you plan to create — which helps it show
your posts to the right audience later.
Step 3: Avoid Spammy Behavior
Don’t go wild:
Don’t follow 50+ people in one day.
3
Don’t like 100 videos back-to-back.
Don’’t Repeat the same Comment on every video
These are red flags that make Platform ban your account.
Instead:
Keep engagement natural and spaced out.
--- صفحة 56 ---
step 4 — Draft Before You Post
After 2-3 days of warm-up, upload 5–6 videos and save them as drafts.
This signals to the platform that you are preparing to become an active creator.
It establishes intent, which helps unlock early distribution potential.
4
Step 5 — Begin Posting with Strategy
Start uploading content after your warm-up phase:
DAY#1 = AFTER THE 3-DAYS WARMING, START UPLOAD THE FIRST VIDEO ON THE
ACCOUNT.
DAY#2 = NO POSTING, JUST SCROLL AND WARM-UP
DAY#3 = UPLOAD TWO VIDEOS ONLY.
5 DAY#4 = NO POSTING, JUST SCROLL AND WARM-UP
DAY#5 = UPLOAD ONE VIDEO ONLY.
DAY#6 = UPLOAD TWO VIDEOS ONLY.
DAY#7 = NO POSTING, JUST SCROLL AND WARM-UP
AFTER THIS
Post 1–2 times per day.
Leave at least 2 hours between each post.
Maintain Uploading consistency as Daily basis until the Account Healthy become
great and after this you can increase your uploading to 3-5 videos/D
This creates a stable foundation for growth without overwhelming the account.
Step 6 — Avoid These Early Mistakes
Do not use any hashtags on your first 4-5 videos.
Do not delete any videos, even if they perform poorly.
Deleting early videos sends negative signals to the algorithm and may reduce your
visibility. 6
Additional Tips for Long-Term Success
Reply to comments to encourage engagement and show activity.
Spend 15–30 minutes per day simply scrolling and interacting with your FYP.
Keep producing — consistency is more powerful than perfection early on.

⚠ NOTE:
Most People Fail Because of Content — Not Setup
Even if everything technical is done right, the content strategy is what
makes or breaks your account.
👉 Each account — especially on the same platform — should focus on
a different type of content to avoid overlap and boost reach.
Example Breakdown:
Account 1: Reactions
Acc ount 2: Motivational clips
Account 3: Educational/value-based content
✅ This makes each account unique, engaging a wider range of
audience types while staying within the same personal brand.
--- صفحة 82 ---
Step-by-Step Instructions
✅ 1. Plan Branding & Naming for Each Account
Start by choosing a username and content angle for each account.
Each account — even on the same platform — should have a unique
content focus.
Examples of account styles:
Moosama-Clips → Reaction videos
Moosama-Talks → Motivational content
Best of Mo Osama → Educational or high-value tips
Moosama-Lifestyle → Daily routines, behind-the-scenes
Moosama-Mindset → Self-improvement clips
Moosama-Network → Interviews, networking clips
✅ 2. Prepare Platform-Specific Emails
Use a separate email for each Platform. {OPTIONAL}
Keep access to every email for verification purposes.
✅ 3. Create the Account
Open the account using the assigned email.
Set Your Different username, bio, and profile picture based on the
branding plan.
✅ 4. Configure Account Settings
Change the country/region to suit the audience.
Go to settings:
Add and verify phone number
Add and verify email
Switch from personal to business account
--- صفحة 86 ---
Step 1: Don’t Rush It
New account? Wait.
For the first 1–2 days, don’t post anything.
Just behave like a normal user:
1
Watch videos.
Like some (5–10 per session).
Leave a few genuine comments.
Follow 1–5 creators in your niche.
Repeat this activity daily for at least 2 days or from beginning of open the
account (30+ minutes per day)
Step 2: Stay Inside Your Niche
Engage ONLY with content related to your niche.
If you're planning to post:
2
Fitness content? Watch fitness clips.
Finance tips? Interact with finance creators.
Comedy or reactions? Stick with those.
This tells what kind of content you plan to create — which helps it show
your posts to the right audience later.
Step 3: Avoid Spammy Behavior
Don’t go wild:
Don’t follow 50+ people in one day.
3
Don’t like 100 videos back-to-back.
Don’’t Repeat the same Comment on every video
These are red flags that make Platform ban your account.
Instead:
Keep engagement natural and spaced out.
--- صفحة 87 ---
step 4 — Draft Before You Post
After 2-3 days of warm-up, upload 5–6 videos and save them as drafts.
This signals to the platform that you are preparing to become an active creator.
It establishes intent, which helps unlock early distribution potential.
4
Step 5 — Begin Posting with Strategy
Start uploading content after your warm-up phase:
DAY#1 = AFTER THE 3-DAYS WARMING, START UPLOAD THE FIRST VIDEO ON THE
ACCOUNT.
DAY#2 = NO POSTING, JUST SCROLL AND WARM-UP
DAY#3 = UPLOAD TWO VIDEOS ONLY.
5 DAY#4 = NO POSTING, JUST SCROLL AND WARM-UP
DAY#5 = UPLOAD ONE VIDEO ONLY.
DAY#6 = UPLOAD TWO VIDEOS ONLY.
DAY#7 = NO POSTING, JUST SCROLL AND WARM-UP
AFTER THIS
Post 1–2 times per day.
Leave at least 2 hours between each post.
Maintain Uploading consistency as Daily basis until the Account Healthy become
great and after this you can increase your uploading to 3-5 videos/D
This creates a stable foundation for growth without overwhelming the account.
Step 6 — Avoid These Early Mistakes
Do not use any hashtags on your first 4-5 videos.
Do not delete any videos, even if they perform poorly.
Deleting early videos sends negative signals to the algorithm and may reduce your
visibility. 6
Additional Tips for Long-Term Success
Reply to comments to encourage engagement and show activity.
Spend 15–30 minutes per day simply scrolling and interacting with your FYP.
Keep producing — consistency is more powerful than perfection early on.

✅ On-Camera Appearance Guidelines
1. Clothing
Wear clean, neat, and visually pleasant clothing
Choose solid colors or soft tones — avoid loud patterns or flashy designs
Clothing should reflect professionalism and trust (e.g., plain shirt, blazer, or simple t-shirt
depending on brand tone)
2. Grooming
Make sure you are well-groomed before recording, If you have facial hair, shave or trim it
neatly to maintain a clean and trustworthy look
✅ Lighting Guidelines
Create a clean, bright, and professional look
Eliminate shadows on the face and background distractions
Use PRO MIC if you have....

--- صفحة 100 ---
HOW TO SET-UP YOUR
PRO EMAILS
IMAP {(Internet Message Access Protocol)
Receives and syncs emails across multiple devices.
Stores emails on the server, so you can access them
from anywhere.
Any action (read, delete, move) is reflected across all
connected devices.
SMTP (Simple Mail Transfer Protocol)
Sends emails from your email client to the recipient’s
server.
Does not store emails—it only transfers them.
Requires authentication (email & password) for
security.

1. EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
1.1 Company Overview
Fluxa Media is a specialized Personal Brand Distribution Agency focused on transforming
content creators — specifically podcasters — into dominant niche authorities through strategic
content distribution and viral growth systems .
Founded : December 2025
Founder : Moaz
Location : Egypt ( serving global markets )
Legal Structure : Sole Proprietorship ( transitioning to LLC by Month 6  
Industry : Digital Marketing , Content Distribution , Personal Branding
1.2 The Problem We Solve
High - quality content creators face a critical challenge : reach stagnation . Despite producing
excellent content consistently , their growth plateaus due to :
Algorithm limitations on single accounts
Lack of multi - platform distribution strategy
--- صفحة 149 ---
No systematic approach to viral content extraction
Limited understanding of platform - specific optimization
Time constraints preventing consistent posting
Inability to scale content production internally
This creates a " quality - reach gap " where exceptional content fails to achieve proportional
  24  
visibility and business impact .
1.3 Our Solution
Fluxa Media operates a Content Distribution Growth Machine that delivers :
Core Service Components :
      Strategic Audience Research - Deep analysis of client ' s niche , competitors , and audience
psychology
      Content Strategy Development - 30   40 monthly content angles designed for virality
      Viral Moment Extraction - Professional team identifies high - potential clips from long - form
content
      Multi - Platform Editing - Platform - optimized editing following proven viral frameworks
      Mass Distribution System - 6   9 secondary accounts posting 2,000   4,500 videos monthly
      Performance Analytics - Weekly reports and monthly strategy optimization
Guaranteed Results :
100 M + organic views within 4   5 months
3   10 X increase in sales / lead generation
Established authority positioning in client ' s niche
Systematic , predictable growth trajectory
1.4 Target Market
Primary Focus : English - speaking podcasters in North America and Europe
Ideal Client Profile :
YouTube subscribers : 50,000   800,000
Content categories : Business , Self - improvement , Health , Finance
Current monthly revenue : $ 10,000   $ 100,000
Pain point : Stagnant reach despite quality content
Willingness to invest : $ 5,000   $ 15,000/ month
Market Size : 5,000+ qualified prospects in target range , representing a $ 250 M + addressable
market annually .
--- صفحة 150 ---
1.5 Business Model
Revenue Model : Monthly Recurring Revenue   MRR ) through retainer - based service contracts
Pricing Tiers :
Foundation Package : $ 5,000/ month   6 accounts , 2,000 videos / month )
Growth Package : $ 8,000/ month   9 accounts , 3,000 videos / month )
Authority Package : $ 13,000/ month   12 accounts , 4,500 videos / month )
Contract Terms : 3- month minimum commitment , paid monthly , no refunds ( clear deliverables
and KPIs )
1.6 Financial Projections
Period Clients Monthly Revenue Annual Run Rate
Month 3 2   3 $ 13,000 $ 156,000
Month 6 5   6 $ 35,000 $ 420,000
Month 12 8   10 $ 65,000 $ 780,000

1.7 Competitive Advantage
Unlike traditional video editing services or general marketing agencies , Fluxa Media offers :
      Specialized Niche Focus - Deep expertise in podcast content distribution
  24  
      Proven System - Based on strategies used by Joe Rogan , Iman Gadzhi , Andrew Tate
      Mass Distribution - 2,000   4,500 videos / month vs . industry standard of 20   50
      Full - Service Model - From strategy to execution , not just editing
      Performance Guarantee - 100 M views or continued service until achieved
      Technical Excellence - Proprietary anti - shadowban systems and local distribution
infrastructure
1.8 Funding Requirements
Bootstrapped Model : Zero external funding required .
Strategy : Use first client ' s payment to fund team , reinvest profits for growth .
Capital Requirements :
Month 1   2   $ 0 ( pre - revenue , founder does sales )

Month 6   $ 5,000 ( scaling operations )

2. COMPANY OVERVIEW
2.1 Mission Statement
" To democratize personal brand growth by providing world - class content distribution systems
that transform quality creators into niche authorities , regardless of their starting audience size ."
2.2 Vision Statement
" To become the #1 recognized Personal Brand Distribution Agency globally , known for
delivering 100 M + views and 10 X business growth for every client we serve ."
2.3 Core Values
1. Results Over Promises
We measure success by client metrics , not our own effort
Every strategy is data - driven and tested
Transparency in reporting and communication
2. Systematic Excellence
SOPs for every process
Quality control at every stage
Continuous improvement through analytics
3. Client Success First
Their growth is our growth
Long - term partnerships over short - term gains
Proactive strategy adjustments
4. Speed of Execution
48- hour onboarding maximum
Weekly tangible deliverables
--- صفحة 152 ---
Real - time problem resolution
5. Innovation in Distribution
Constantly testing new platforms
Adapting to algorithm changes
Pioneering growth techniques
2.4 Company History & Foundation
Founding Story :
Fluxa Media was founded based on firsthand observation of a critical market gap : exceptionally
talented content creators struggling to achieve reach proportional to their content quality .
The founding insight came from studying successful personal brands like Joe Rogan , Iman
Gadzhi , and Andrew Tate , who all utilized secondary account distribution strategies to
  24  
achieve exponential growth . However , this strategy remained largely unknown or
inaccessible to mid - tier creators due to :
Technical complexity ( avoiding shadowbans , managing multiple accounts )
Resource intensity ( requires full team and systems )
Knowledge barrier ( understanding platform algorithms and viral mechanics )
Fluxa Media was created to productize this proven growth system and make it accessible to
serious content creators through a full - service agency model .
2.5 Legal Structure
Current : Sole Proprietorship   Month 1   6  
Simple setup , minimal overhead
Owner retains full control
Suitable for early validation phase
Planned : Limited Liability Company   LLC ) by Month 6
Asset protection
Tax optimization
Professional credibility for larger clients
Preparation for scaling and potential partnerships
Jurisdiction :
Primary operations : Egypt ( cost efficiency )
Client serving : Global   USA , UK , Canada , Germany , Australia focus )
Future consideration : Delaware LLC or UK Ltd for international credibility

  24  

2. Retention Engineering   Throughout )

3. Caption System
Style : Dynamic , word - by - word or phrase - by - phrase
Readability : High contrast , large font , positioned top - third
Emphasis : Color changes or animations on key words
Accessibility : Accurate transcription for deaf / hard - of - hearing viewers
4. Platform - Specific Optimization
TikTok : Fast - paced , trend - aware , music / sounds from TikTok library
Instagram Reels : Slightly slower , aesthetic focus , trending audio
YouTube Shorts : Educational tone , longer retention acceptable , clear value
5. Branding   Subtle  
Intro : No logo ( kills retention ), just straight into content

Watermark : Small , unobtrusive logo in corner ( optional )
  24  

  24  

Most freelancers and small agencies can ' t afford pre - revenue investment

Requires extensive SOPs , quality control , project management

Our systems ( once built ) are proprietary and complex to replicate

7. MARKETING & SALES STRATEGY
7.1 Go - To - Market Strategy
Phase 1   Month 1   3     Direct Outbound Sales
Primary Channel : Cold Email Outreach
Why Email First :
Low cost ( essentially free )
Scalable ( can send 100   200/ day )
Trackable ( open rates , reply rates , conversions )
Async ( doesn ' t require real - time engagement )
Professional context ( podcasters expect business inquiries )
Email Strategy :
List Building :
Source : YouTube search , Spotify charts , podcast directories
Criteria : 50 K   800 K subscribers , English - speaking , business / health / finance niches
Tool : Manual research + spreadsheet   Month 1   , then VA assistance   Month 2    
Target : 50 new leads per week = 200/ month
  24  
Email Structure ( based on Mohamed Osama framework ) :
--- صفحة 177 ---
Subject: [Personalized question about their podcast]
[Ice Breaker - specific observation about their content]
[Strategic Question - identify their pain point]
[Bold Claim - 100M views in 5 months]
[Social Proof - case studies from niche]
[Reverse Pain - what they're missing by not distributing properly]
[Solution Bridge - our system briefly]
[CTA - book 20-minute call or watch Loom]
Follow - Up Sequence :
Day 0   Initial email
Day 3   Follow - up #1 ( add value - share insight about their niche )
Day 7   Follow - up #2 ( case study attachment )
Day 14   Follow - up #3 ( final check - in with urgency )
Day 21   Break - up email (" Assuming you ' re not interested , but ...")
Conversion Funnel :
100 emails sent
30   40% open rate = 30   40 opens
5   10% reply rate = 5   10 replies
50% call booking rate = 2   5 calls
20   30% close rate = 0.5   1.5 clients per 100 emails
Therefore : Sending 100 emails / week = 1   2 clients / month ( conservative )
Phase 2   Month 4   6     Multi - Channel Outbound
Channel 2   LinkedIn Outreach
Target : Business podcasters , coaches , consultants active on LinkedIn
Strategy :
Send connection request with personalized note
Once connected , send value - first message ( insight about their content )
Share case study or Loom video
Invite to discovery call
Volume : 30   50 connection requests / week
--- صفحة 178 ---
Channel 3   Loom Video Outreach
Strategy :
Record 5   10 minute Loom analyzing prospect ' s content
Identify specific opportunities they ' re missing
Share link via email or LinkedIn
Highly personalized , stands out from text - only outreach
Volume : 5   10 Loom videos / week ( targeted at high - value prospects )
Channel 4   TikTok / Instagram Engagement
Strategy :
Comment genuinely on prospects ' content
Provide value in comments ( not salesy )
Build rapport over 2   3 weeks
DM with offer
Volume : Engage with 10   20 prospects / day
Phase 3   Month 7   12     Inbound Marketing

Tactics :
LinkedIn Posts   3 x / week ): Case studies , growth insights , industry trends
Twitter / X Threads   2 x / week ): Tactical tips , viral breakdowns
YouTube Channel   1 x / week ): Behind - the - scenes , client success stories , education
Newsletter   1 x / week ): Email list building , nurture sequence
Referral Program :
Structure :
Existing clients get $ 1,000 credit for each qualified referral who signs
Referred client gets first month at $ 500 discount
Implement in Month 4 ( once we have 2   3 happy clients )

Podcast hosting platforms   Spotify for Creators , etc .)

7.2 Sales Process
Lead Qualification :
Before booking call , prospect must meet :
Fit Criteria :
50 K + audience
English - speaking
Business / monetization focus
Budget capacity   $ 5 K   / month )
Discovery Call Structure   30   40 Minutes ):
Minute 0   5   Rapport Building
How did you start your podcast ?
What ' s been your journey so far ?
What made you successful initially ?
Minute 5   15   Problem Discovery
How ' s growth been recently ?   Identify plateau )
What have you tried to accelerate growth ?   Qualify seriousness )
What ' s frustrating about your current situation ?   Emotional pain )
Where do you want to be in 6   12 months ?   Vision and goals )
Minute 15   25   Solution Presentation
" Here ' s what we do differently ..."   Explain secondary account strategy )
Share case study relevant to their niche
Walk through our process ( onboarding to results )
Show example report / analytics
Minute 25   30   Pricing & Objection Handling
Present tiered pricing
Explain guarantee
Address objections ( pre - empt common ones )
Minute 30   35   Close
" Based on what you ' ve shared , I think the   X ] package is right fit . Want to move forward ?"
If yes : Send contract and onboarding link
--- صفحة 180 ---
If " need to think ": Schedule follow - up call in 3   5 days
If objections : Handle and reassess
Post - Call :
Send thank - you email with :
Proposal PDF ( pricing , deliverables , guarantee )
Case study deck
Contract link   PandaDoc or HelloSign )
FAQ document
Follow up in 2   3 days if no response
Common Objections & Handling :
Objection 1   " Seems expensive "
Response :
" I understand - $ 5,000/ month is an investment . Let me ask : if we achieve the 100 M views in 5
months , and that brings you even 10 new high - ticket clients at $ 3 K each , that ' s $ 30 K in revenue
from a $ 25 K investment . Most of our clients see 3   10 X ROI . Does that math work for your
business ?"
Objection 2   " How do I know this will work for my niche ?"

  Short-Form Video Editor Needed (TikTok/Instagram/YouTube Shorts)
About Us:
Fluxa Media - Agency helping creators go viral with 100M+ views.
Your Role:
- Edit 5-10 short videos daily (15-60 seconds each)
- Follow strict editing standards (hooks, retention, captions, SFX)
- Schedule posts on social media
- Work with our Team Leader
Requirements:
- Expert in Premiere Pro / DaVinci / Final Cut
- Portfolio of short-form content (TikTok/Reels style)
- Fast turnaround (ability to edit 5-10 videos/day)
- Understands viral content mechanics
- Available 8 hours/day, 6 days/week
Compensation: $300-$500/month (based on speed & quality)
To Apply:
1. Send portfolio (10 short-form videos you edited)
2. Complete test: Edit this [sample clip] in TikTok viral style
3. Tell us: How many videos can you edit per day?

26.1 ( ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د 45 - 35 ) ﺔ ﻤ ﻟ ﺎ ﻜ ﻤ ﻟ ا ﻞ ﻜ ﻴ ﻫ
5 - 0 ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د : Rapport Building

5 - 0 ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د   Rapport
"Hi [Name], thanks for hopping on. How's your day going?
Great. I was just listening to [specific episode] - loved your take on [specific point].
Quick question before we dive in: what's been the biggest win from your podcast so far?"
15 - 5 ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د   Problem Discovery
"Tell me about your growth journey. When did you start noticing things plateau?
What have you tried to accelerate reach? Editors? Agencies? DIY?
What's the most frustrating part right now?
Where do you want to be in 6 months? What would 'winning' look like?"
--- صفحة 267 ---
25 - 15 ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د   Solution
"Perfect. Here's what we do differently:
Most agencies edit 20-50 videos/month and post to your main account.
We do 2,000-4,500 videos/month across 9 secondary accounts.
[Share screen - show account structure diagram]
The math: 3,000 videos × 50K average views = 150M views/5 months.
We guarantee 100M organic views or we keep working.
Want me to walk you through a sample strategy for your niche?"
35 - 25 ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د   Pricing
"Based on your goals, I recommend 3,000 videos/month.
Investment: $7,500/month for 3 months minimum.
Includes: [list everything]
Most clients see 5-10X ROI through leads/sales.
Does this fit your budget?"
40 - 35 ﺔ ﻘ ﻴ ﻗ د   Close
"Great. Next step: send over the onboarding form and first payment.
I'll personally handle your onboarding and strategy call.
Ready to get started? I can send the contract now."
